        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2572633707" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3624077241162583838">The description of this story led me to believe that this was going to be about Batman being the bad guy and Joker being the good guy. I was really excited about that but, unfortunately, it's not really about that at all. Basically, the Joker becomes a lot less of an asshole, and Batman becomes a lot more of an asshole. Batman is still trying to save the day (and being a major jerk about it), and Joker is still unleashing terror on the city (but he's just so swell now). <br/><br/>There are also two Harley</span>
  <span id="freeText3624077241162583838" style="display:none">The description of this story led me to believe that this was going to be about Batman being the bad guy and Joker being the good guy. I was really excited about that but, unfortunately, it's not really about that at all. Basically, the Joker becomes a lot less of an asshole, and Batman becomes a lot more of an asshole. Batman is still trying to save the day (and being a major jerk about it), and Joker is still unleashing terror on the city (but he's just so swell now). <br /><br />There are also two Harley Quinns now, and one of them is also "Neo Joker". It's not as complicated as it sounds, but it is as contrived as it sounds. <br /><br />The worst part of this story, though, is how it tries to wrap up all of its various plot points and side stories in the last few pages. <br /><br />Despite these complaints, this wasn't terrible. It wasn't the story that I thought I was getting, but it was fine for what it was. The art was also really nice. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3624077241162583838" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('6cAbfx1gr5DthGMH44LpLNhEHjmZJp9/3mVJpn4a9G96fe76Y+eBklDQvCI0VhLuFmYWhqhf9HbUJYSZ/vW/5g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Qg9oDMCd2LF+SqaKTnSEhVdJ01lTFeKUhtyA3g61zhbRsp2Jvhr2s8Meea+ZoH9HmWvb5mJsiZ2MnE3hjlqFnw==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer10911109110401541530">After breaking into the industry at a young age, Sean Murphy made a name for himself in the world of indie comics before joining up with DC. In his tenure, he has worked on such titles as <i>Batman/Scarecrow: Year One</i>, <i>Teen Titans</i>, <i>Hellblazer</i>, <i>Joe The Barbarian</i>, and the critically acclaimed miniseries <i>American Vampire: Survival Of The Fittest</i> and <i>The Wake</i> with Scott Snyder. Murphy also wrote and illu</span>
  <span id="freeText10911109110401541530" style="display:none">After breaking into the industry at a young age, Sean Murphy made a name for himself in the world of indie comics before joining up with DC. In his tenure, he has worked on such titles as <i>Batman/Scarecrow: Year One</i>, <i>Teen Titans</i>, <i>Hellblazer</i>, <i>Joe The Barbarian</i>, and the critically acclaimed miniseries <i>American Vampire: Survival Of The Fittest</i> and <i>The Wake</i> with Scott Snyder. Murphy also wrote and illustrated the original graphic novel <i>Offroad</i> and the popular miniseries <i>Punk Rock Jesus</i>.</span>
